# PakLaw AI Whole-Project Test Cases

This document contains **1,500 whole-project test cases** covering the implemented Next.js frontend, Firebase Authentication, Firestore rules, browser persistence, and the planned FastAPI, ingestion, ChromaDB, retrieval, LegalBERT NLI, consistency-reasoning, explainability, monitoring, and deployment architecture.

## Test Conventions

* **H**: Critical path, security, authentication, data loss, or blocking failure.
* **M**: Important behavior, validation, persistence, or usability.
* **L**: Presentation, polish, or lower-risk compatibility behavior.
* **Status**: `Pass`, `Fail`, or `To Be Tested`. All cases default to `To Be Tested` until formally executed.
* Firebase-dependent cases require a configured test Firebase project and test accounts.
* File tests should use harmless sample files containing no confidential information.
* Repository contents are metadata stored in browser `localStorage`; document binary contents are not persisted.
* Analysis and report data are currently simulated in the frontend. Frontend cases validate the implemented UI contract.
* Backend, NLI, ingestion, vector database, and deployment cases are architecture-level acceptance/contract tests to execute as those components are implemented.

## Coverage Summary

|Area|Cases|
|-|-:|
|Login, Signup, Verification, and Reset|100|
|Session State and Protected Routes|90|
|Dashboard, Navbar, Footer, and Theme|90|

|Multi-File Analysis|100|
|Federal Statutes Search|90|
|Analysis Report|90|
|Profile|90|
|Settings and Account Changes|90|
|Accessibility, Responsive UI, Security, and Resilience|100|
|Backend API and FastAPI Contracts|30|
|Data Ingestion and Corpus Validation|30|
|Preprocessing and Legal Parsing|30|
|Knowledge Representation and Graph|30|
|Embeddings and ChromaDB|30|
|Retrieval and Reranking|30|
|NLI Model Inference|30|
|Consistency Reasoner|30|
|Explanation, Citations, and Reports|30|
|Document Upload, PDF, and Text Extraction|30|
|Backend Security and Access Control|30|
|Performance, Concurrency, and Reliability|30|
|Configuration, Docker, and Deployment|30|
|Logging, Audit, and Model Monitoring|30|
|End-to-End System Integration|30|
|**Total**|**1500**|

## 1\. Login, Signup, Verification, and Reset

|ID|Scenario|Steps / Test Data|Expected Result|Priority|Status|
|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|TC-0001|Login page initial render|Open `/login` while signed out.|Brand, email, password, reset link, sign-in button, and signup link render without layout errors.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0002|Valid verified-user login|Enter a verified account email and correct password; submit.|Sign-in succeeds and the user reaches `/`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0003|Unverified-user login|Enter valid credentials for an unverified account.|Login is rejected, Firebase session is ended, and verification guidance is shown.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0004|Wrong password|Enter a registered email and incorrect password.|User remains signed out and sees a friendly invalid-credential message.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0005|Unknown email|Enter an unregistered valid-format email and any password.|User remains signed out and receives a non-crashing authentication error.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0006|Invalid email syntax|Enter `not-an-email` and a password.|Native or Firebase validation prevents successful login.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0007|Empty email|Leave email empty, enter password, and submit.|Browser required-field validation blocks submission.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0008|Empty password|Enter email, leave password empty, and submit.|Browser required-field validation blocks submission.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0009|Login loading state|Submit valid credentials on a throttled connection.|Button becomes disabled and displays `Signing in...` until completion.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0010|Duplicate login submission|Rapidly activate the submit button after the first submission.|Disabled loading state prevents accidental repeated submissions.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0011|Login network failure|Disable network before submitting valid credentials.|A friendly network error is displayed and the page remains usable.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0012|Too many login attempts|Trigger Firebase rate limiting with repeated failed attempts.|The user sees the mapped retry-later message.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0013|Authenticated user opens login|Open `/login` with an authenticated verified session.|The page redirects to `/` using route replacement.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0014|Forgot-password navigation|Select `Forgot password?` on login.|Browser navigates to `/forgot-password`.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0015|Signup navigation|Select `Create one` on login.|Browser navigates to `/signup`.|L|To Be Tested|
|TC-0016|Signup page initial render|Open `/signup`.|All four fields, terms checkbox, submit button, and sign-in link render correctly.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0017|Successful signup|Enter a unique email, name, matching password of 6+ characters, accept terms, and submit.|Account is created, verification is requested, user is signed out, and inbox screen appears.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0018|Signup stores profile|Complete signup and inspect the test account/profile document.|Display name and user profile fields are written when Firebase operations succeed.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0019|Signup duplicate email|Submit an email already registered.|Signup is rejected with the mapped email-in-use message.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0020|Signup password mismatch|Enter different password and confirmation values.|No Firebase request is made and `Passwords do not match.` appears.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0021|Signup short password|Enter matching 5-character passwords.|No Firebase request is made and the minimum-length message appears.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0022|Signup terms not accepted|Complete all fields but leave terms unchecked.|Browser validation blocks submission.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0023|Signup required fields|Attempt submission with each required field empty in turn.|The corresponding field is identified and signup does not proceed.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0024|Signup loading state|Submit valid signup data on a throttled connection.|Button is disabled and displays `Creating account...`.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0025|Signup completion email display|Complete signup with `person@example.com`.|Completion screen shows the submitted email accurately and offers sign-in navigation.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0026|Reset known email|Submit a registered email on `/forgot-password`.|A reset request is sent and the generic inbox screen is shown.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0027|Reset unknown email privacy|Submit an unregistered email.|The same generic inbox screen appears without revealing account existence.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0028|Reset malformed email privacy|Cause Firebase `invalid-email` handling.|The generic completion response is shown without account disclosure.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0029|Reset service failure|Simulate an unmapped Firebase or network error.|A generic retry message appears and the form remains available.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0030|Reset navigation|Use both `Return to Sign In` controls before and after submission.|Each control navigates to `/login`.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0031|Login page initial render - variant 11|Open `/login` while signed out. Run test on offline status transition using a test account on gmail.com.|System handles 'login page initial render' correctly for 'offline status transition' without crash, data loss, unauthorized access, or incorrect navigation.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0032|Edge case: Valid verified-user login with input variations|Execute 'Valid verified-user login' scenario with special characters, trailing spaces, or mixed-case identifiers. Steps: Enter a verified account email and correct password; submit.|Sanitizers strip trailing spaces; authentication behaves case-insensitively for email fields.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0033|Security check: Unverified-user login session isolation|Execute 'Unverified-user login' while checking session storage keys and cookie updates. Steps: Enter valid credentials for an unverified account.|No token leak or credential caching is visible in cookies or logs.|H|To Be Tested|

## 2\. Session State and Protected Routes

|ID|Scenario|Steps / Test Data|Expected Result|Priority|Status|
|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|TC-0101|Auth startup loading|Open the app while Firebase is restoring a session.|Protected content does not flash before auth state resolves.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0102|Signed-out dashboard access|Open `/` without a session.|Loading message appears briefly, then browser redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0103|Signed-out check access|Open `/check` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`; audit form is not exposed.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0104|Signed-out repositories access|Open `/repositories` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`; repository data is not displayed.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0105|Signed-out multi-analysis access|Open `/multi-analysis` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0106|Signed-out search access|Open `/search` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0107|Signed-out report access|Open `/report` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0108|Signed-out profile access|Open `/profile` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0109|Signed-out settings access|Open `/settings` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0110|Signed-out password-change access|Open `/change-password` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0111|Signed-out email-change access|Open `/change-email` without a session.|Page redirects to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0112|Verified session refresh|Log in, refresh a protected page, and wait for Firebase restoration.|Session is restored and the same protected page becomes available.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0113|Unverified persisted Firebase user|Restore an unverified Firebase user state.|Application treats the user as unauthenticated and protected routes remain blocked.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0114|Session sign-out propagation|Sign out from one tab and focus another open protected tab.|Firebase auth change clears application identity and protected content becomes inaccessible.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0115|Firestore profile read failure|Simulate failure while loading the signed-in user's profile.|Auth data fallback supplies name/email and app remains usable.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0116|Missing Firestore profile|Sign in with a verified Firebase account lacking a user document.|User is still authenticated using Firebase Auth profile data.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0117|Missing Firebase display name|Sign in with no display name and no readable user profile.|Safe fallback name `User` is used.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0118|Refresh user after verification|Verify an account, invoke auth refresh, and reload session state.|Verified user is built and authenticated state becomes available.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0119|Logout state cleanup|Log out from the navbar.|Auth user and Firebase user state clear and browser navigates to `/login`.|H|To Be Tested|

## 4\. Single Consistency Audit

|ID|Scenario|Steps / Test Data|Expected Result|Priority|Status|
|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|TC-0281|Audit page render|Open `/check` authenticated.|Repository selector, text area, voice button, drop zone, and analysis button render.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0282|Default knowledge base|Open the page with repositories available.|Selector defaults to `None` and explains that all Pak Law PDFs will be scanned.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0283|Repository options|Create empty and populated repositories, then open `/check`.|Every repository appears with accurate empty/file-count text.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0284|Select repository|Choose a repository from the selector.|Selection remains visible and scope guidance changes to selected-repository wording.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0285|Return to global scope|Select a repository, then choose `None`.|Global-scope explanation returns.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0286|Text-only audit|Enter non-whitespace draft text and submit.|Loading state starts and browser navigates to `/report` after the simulated delay.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0287|PDF-only audit|Upload valid PDF under 10 MB with empty text; submit.|File is accepted and audit proceeds.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0288|DOC-only audit|Upload valid `.doc` under 10 MB.|File name appears and text is no longer required.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0289|DOCX-only audit|Upload valid `.docx` under 10 MB.|File is accepted.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0290|TXT-only audit|Upload valid `.txt` under 10 MB.|File is accepted.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0291|Text and file audit|Provide text and a valid file, then submit.|Both inputs coexist and audit proceeds once.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0292|Empty submission|Submit without meaningful text or a file.|Error requests draft text or a document and no navigation occurs.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0293|Whitespace-only text|Enter spaces/newlines only and submit.|Client validation treats input as empty and does not analyze.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0294|Exactly 10 MB file|Upload an accepted file exactly 10 MB.|File is accepted.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0295|File above 10 MB|Upload an accepted file larger than 10 MB.|File is cleared and size-limit error appears.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0296|Unsupported extension and MIME|Upload `.exe` or `.png`.|File is rejected and accepted-format error appears.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0297|Accepted extension with blank MIME|Upload a valid `.pdf` whose browser reports no MIME.|Extension fallback accepts the file.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0298|Uppercase extension|Upload `STATUTE.PDF`.|Case-insensitive extension validation accepts it.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0299|Misleading unsupported extension|Upload `law.pdf.exe`.|File is rejected.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0300|Drop valid file|Drag a valid file over the drop zone and release it.|Active styling appears during drag and file is selected on drop.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0301|Drop invalid file|Drop an unsupported file.|Active styling clears, file is rejected, and error is displayed.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0302|Drag leave|Drag a file over and then out of the zone.|Active drag styling clears without selecting a file.|L|To Be Tested|
|TC-0303|Click file picker|Click the drop zone.|Hidden file picker opens and filters advertised extensions.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0304|Replace selected file|Select one valid file, then select another.|Displayed selection changes to the latest valid file.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0305|Invalid replacement clears prior file|Select valid file, then choose invalid file.|Previous selection is cleared and error is shown.|H|To Be Tested|

|ID|Scenario|Steps / Test Data|Expected Result|Priority|Status|

## 11\. Accessibility, Responsive UI, Security, and Resilience

|ID|Scenario|Steps / Test Data|Expected Result|Priority|Status|
|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|TC-0951|Keyboard page navigation|Navigate each page using Tab and Shift+Tab only.|Interactive controls are reachable in a logical order.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0952|Visible keyboard focus|Tab through links, buttons, inputs, filters, and modal controls.|Focus location is visibly identifiable.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0953|Enter/Space activation|Activate buttons, checkboxes, dropdown trigger, and links by keyboard.|Controls perform the same action as pointer activation.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0954|Form label association|Inspect login, signup, audit, repository, settings, email, and password forms.|Labels correctly target their inputs and screen readers announce purpose.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0955|Mobile layout at 320 px|Test every route at 320 px width.|No essential content is clipped; actions remain operable.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0956|Tablet layout|Test at 768 px width.|Grids, cards, menus, forms, and modals adapt without overlap.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0957|Wide desktop layout|Test at 1440 px and above.|Content remains centered/readable and does not stretch excessively.|L|To Be Tested|
|TC-0958|Browser zoom 200%|Zoom each key workflow to 200%.|Content reflows, controls remain reachable, and text does not overlap.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0959|Long-name layout|Use an 80-character display/repository/file name.|Text truncates or wraps without breaking navbar/cards.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0960|Modal viewport containment|Open search/report modal on a short mobile viewport.|Modal content remains accessible and does not trap unreachable controls.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0961|Dark-theme contrast|Inspect text, inputs, cards, errors, success messages, and badges in dark mode.|Content remains legible with distinguishable states.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0962|Light-theme contrast|Inspect the same elements in light mode.|Content remains legible with distinguishable states.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0963|Error announcement visibility|Trigger every form/file error.|Error appears near the relevant workflow with clear wording and no layout shift that hides controls.|M|To Be Tested|
|TC-0964|LocalStorage malformed repository JSON|Store invalid JSON under the signed-in user's repository key and reload.|Context catches parsing failure and safely shows an empty repository list.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0965|LocalStorage unavailable|Block localStorage access and open theme/repository/profile workflows.|App should fail gracefully; any uncaught exception is recorded as a defect.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0966|Stored repository schema corruption|Store parseable but malformed repository data and open affected pages.|App should avoid crashing; missing schema validation is recorded if rendering fails.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0967|User-generated text rendering|Use repository/profile names containing `<script>`, HTML, quotes, and ampersands.|React renders text literally; no script executes or HTML is injected.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0968|Firebase configuration failure|Start frontend with missing/invalid public Firebase configuration.|Failure is detectable and no misleading authenticated state is shown.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0969|Rapid route switching|Move quickly among dashboard, repositories, check, multi-analysis, search, and report.|No stale timer, state update, crash, or cross-page data leak occurs.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0970|Production frontend smoke test|Build/start production frontend and visit every current route.|All routes load without console-breaking errors, missing chunks, or unavailable navigation.|H|To Be Tested|
|TC-0971|Keyboard page navigation - compliance target (WCAG 2.1 AA contrast)|Test 'Keyboard page navigation' to satisfy 'WCAG 2.1 AA contrast' requirements using 'keyboard only'. Steps: Navigate each page using Tab and Shift+Tab only.|All elements comply with 'WCAG 2.1 AA contrast'. Interface navigation is successfully validated on 'keyboard only'.|H|To Be Tested|
